<script>
    $(function(){
        let $scope = $('#account-form_select-icon-popup'),
            popupObject = $('.window:first', $scope).data('object.popup');
            document_selectedIconEvent = 'account-form-popup:icon-selected';

        const Tabs = function() {
            const $tabs = $('.select-tabs:first', $scope);

            $('> a', $tabs).on('click', function(e) {
                $('> a', $tabs).removeClass('selected');
                $(this).addClass('selected');
                $('*[tab-name]', $scope).hide();
                const $tabtoOpen = $('*[tab-name='+$(this).attr('tab-to-open')+']', $scope);
                $tabtoOpen.fadeIn(300);
                e.preventDefault();
                return false;
            });
        }

        const Search = function() {
            let $scopeScope = $('.search:first', $scope),
                $input = $('input[type="text"]:first', $scopeScope),
                searchTerm = '',
                searchURL = '/5363149/configuracoes/contas/new/select_icon',
                delayTimeout;

            $('> a', $scopeScope).on('click', function(e) {
                $(this).toggleClass('active');
                $(this).next().toggle().focus();
                e.preventDefault();
                return false;
            });

            $input.on('keyup', function(e) {
                if ($input.val() != searchTerm) {
                    let $tabInstitutions = $('.tab-institutions:first', $scope);

                    $tabInstitutions.removeClass('loading-content');
                    window.clearTimeout(delayTimeout);
                    delayTimeout = window.setTimeout(function(){
                        $input.attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                        $tabInstitutions.addClass('loading-content');
                        searchTerm = $input.val();
                        $.get(searchURL+'?search='+searchTerm, function(response) {
                            $('> ul', $tabInstitutions).html(response);
                            $tabInstitutions.removeClass('loading-content');
                            $input.attr('disabled', null);
                            $input.focus();
                        });
                    }, 350);
                }
            });
        }

        const IconsList = function() {
            let $iconsLists = $('.popup-content ul', $scope),
                popupObject = $('*[popup-window]:first', $scope).data('object.popup');

            $iconsLists.on('click', 'a', function(e) {
                let $this = $(this)

                $(document).trigger(document_selectedIconEvent, [$this.data('value')]);
                popupObject.close();
                e.preventDefault();
                return false;
            });
        }

        Tabs();
        Search();
        IconsList();
    });
</script>
